Decklists: 9th-32nd
===================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 12, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











While the Top 8 was neatly split between Four-Color Copy Cat and Mardu Ballista/Vehicles one didn't need to look much further to find some variety among the Standard archetypes which did well at Grand Prix Barcelona.







#### Marc Tobiasch's Temur Marvel, 9th at Grand Prix Barcelona 2017


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
